The singer didn’t feel the evil con man should be rewarded for his bad behavior with Peggy Lynn’s virginity, and took action.  The hybrid placed the Professor in time-stream storage and enjoyed her virtue himself.  
Master Red’s travels back to the first half of the Twentieth Century had increased his confidence in the Time/Transport bubble’s reliability, and he was now willing to attempt something much further back.  He knew he had to find a singer to fill in for him while he was out gallivanting around in time, and Peggy Lynn seemed to be the perfect choice.  She was talented enough to handle the job, and it also gave him an opportunity to help her get her career back on track.
After Peggy Lynn accepted his offer, Master knew he was now free to concentrate on giving the time travel function of the TTB Device a real workout.  He began by make a list of the famous people he planned to visit.  The alien scientist had promise that he could have sex with some of the most famous women in history, and he had already sampled a few from the Twentieth Century, but now he intended to go much further back in time and meet some of the legendary beauties he had heard so much about.  It wasn’t the type of situation that came around every day, if at all.  Master felt a tingle in his groin, as he dreamed of taking the virginities of Cleopatra and Joan of Arc.  

The End
